simple media player based on the F\+Fmpeg libraries

A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_acf8113e490f9e7b57465e65af9c0c75c}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx}} should have been set to a device of the specified type before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}!ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}}\index{ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}\label{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+S\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format for a decoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to a suitable frames context inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{doc_2examples_2qsvdec_8c_afe1023087c26d2d410c9cd7d491c8660}{get\+\_\+format()}} callback. The frames context must have been created on a device of the specified type.

When selecting this format for an encoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to the context which will be used for the input frames before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL}!ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}}\index{ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_INTERNAL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa7386da6a6a78eb809d838053e4035ee}\label{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa7386da6a6a78eb809d838053e4035ee}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+AL&The codec supports this format by some internal method.

This format can be selected without any additional configuration -\/ no device or frames context is required. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_FRAME\_CROP\_UNALIGNED@{AV\_FRAME\_CROP\_UNALIGNED}!ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}}\index{ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}!AV\_FRAME\_CROP\_UNALIGNED@{AV\_FRAME\_CROP\_UNALIGNED}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba8df6ec39909b8d97c0a6d2d8465d2e0f}\label{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba8df6ec39909b8d97c0a6d2d8465d2e0f}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+R\+O\+P\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+ED&Apply the maximum possible cropping, even if it requires setting the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}\mbox{]} entries to unaligned pointers. Passing unaligned data to F\+Fmpeg A\+PI is generally not allowed, and causes undefined behavior (such as crashes). You can pass unaligned data only to F\+Fmpeg A\+P\+Is that are explicitly documented to accept it. Use this flag only if you absolutely know what you are doing. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_HWFRAME\_MAP\_READ@{AV\_HWFRAME\_MAP\_READ}!ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}}\index{ffplay.c@{ffplay.c}!AV\_HWFRAME\_MAP\_READ@{AV\_HWFRAME\_MAP\_READ}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba236262031fe4c5503b2611c2c8fb520b}\label{ffplay_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba236262031fe4c5503b2611c2c8fb520b}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{audio\_decode\_frame()}{audio\_decode\_frame()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} audio\+\_\+decode\+\_\+frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_video_state}{Video\+State}} $\ast$}]{is }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Decode one audio frame and return its uncompressed size.

The processed audio frame is decoded, converted if required, and stored in is-\/$>$audio\+\_\+buf, with size in bytes given by the return value.
